śabdaṃ saṃsthāpya ptriśaṅkuṃ mātaṅgarājam idam avocatayaṃ bhos triśaṅko brahmaṇā sahāpatinā cāturmahābhautiko mahāpuruṣaḥ prajñaptaḥ yasyauabśiraḥ satāraṃ gaganam ākāśam udaraṃ tathāucdparvatāś caapy ubhāv ūrū pādau ca dharaṇītalaṃuabsūryācandramasau netre roma tṛṇavanaspatīucdsāgarāś caapy amedhyaṃ vai nadyo sūtrasravo asya tuuabaśrūṇi varṣaṇaṃ cārasya eṣa brahmā sahāpatiḥucdbhavāṃs tu paramajño asi tan me brūhi yathā tathāuiha bhos triśaṅko kim āha svalakṣaṇaṃ brahmaṇaḥ pratyavekṣasvapitrā ca mātrā ca kṛtāni karmāṇi bhavantiaśvastanā stena vañcitāḥuabgacchanti sattvā bahugarbhayoniṃ na caeva kaścin manujo hy ayoniḥucdsamasta jātau pracaranti sattvā na mārutāj jāyate kaścid evauabsvabhāvabhāvyaṃ hy avagaccha loke ke brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrāḥucdsarvatra kāṇāḥ kuṇinaś ca khañjāḥ kuṣṭhī kilāsī hy apasmāriṇo piuabkṛṣṇāś ca gaurāś ca tathāeva śyāmāḥ sattvāḥ prajā hy anyatame viśiṣṭāḥpucdsahaasthicarmāḥ sanakhāḥ samāṃsā duḥkhī sukhī mūtrapurīṣayuktāḥuefna caindriyāṇāṃ praviviktir asti tasmān na varṇāś caturo bhavantiuabmantrair hi yadi labhyeta svargaṃ tu gamanaṃ dvijaḥucdkṛṣṇaśuklāni karmāṇi bhaveyur niṣphalāni hiuefyasmāt kṛṣṇāni śuklāni karmāṇi saphalāni hiughpacyamānāni dṛśyante gatiṣv etāni pañcasuumānavakaśateṣu sa tatra vinihato mahāyaśasā triśaṅkunā puṣkarasārī brāhmaṇo abravītbrāhmaṇo asau mātaṅgarājo hi triśaṅkur nāmabhavān hi brahmā indraś ca kauśikaḥtvam araṇemiś ca gautamaḥtvaṃ śvetaketuś ca śukapaṇḍitaḥvedaḥ samākhyātas tvayā caturdhābhagavān vasūrājarṣir mahāyaśā bhagavānuabjñānena hi tvaṃ parameṇa yuktaḥ svaṣu śāstreṣu bhavān kṛtārthaḥucdśreṣṭho viśiṣṭo paramo asi loke bhavān hi vidyācaraṇena yuktaḥuabdadāmi te ahaṃ prakṛtiṃ mamāmalāṃ śīlena rūpeṇa guṇair upetaḥucdśārdūlakarṇaḥ prakṛtiś ca bhadrā ubhau rametaṃ rucitaṃ mamaidaṃuabpragṛhya bhṛṅgāram udakaprapūrṇam āvarjito brāhmaṇo hṛṣṭacittaḥpucdanupradāsīd udakena kanyakāṃ śārdūlakarṇasya iyam astu bhāryāuudagracitta āsīn mātaṅgarājaḥuabkṛtvā niveśaṃ sa tadātmajasya gatvāāśrame asau nagaraṃ yaśasvīucddharmeṇa vai kārayati svarājyaṃ kṣemaṃ subhikṣaṃ ca sadāutsavaādyaṃ  itiusyād bhikṣavo yuṣmākaṃ kāṅkṣā vā vimatir vā vicikitsā vāanyaḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena triśaṅkur nāma mātaṅgarājo abhūvaṃsyād evaṃ ca bhikṣavo yusmākam anyaḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena śārdūlakarṇā nāma mātaṅgarājakumāro abhūtnaiva draṣṭavyaṃeṣa sa ānando bhikṣuḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena śārdūlakarṇā nāma mātaṅgarājakumāroabhūt syād evaṃ yuṣmākam anyaḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena puṣkarasārī nāma brāhmaṇo abhūtnaiva draṣṭavyaṃeṣa śāradvatīputro bhikṣuḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena puṣkarasārī nāma brāhmaṇo abhūtnaanyā sā tena kālena tena samayena puṣkarasāriṇo brāhmaṇasya prakṛtir nāma māṇavikā duhitāabhūtnaevaṃ draṣṭavyaṃeṣā sā prakṛtir bhikṣuṇī tena kālenatena samayena puṣkarasāriṇo brāhmaṇasya prakṛtir nāma māṇavikā duhitāabhūtsā etarhi p tenaeva snehena tenaeva premṇā anandaṃ bhikṣuṃ gacchantam anugacchati tiṣṭhantam anutiṣṭhatiyad yad eva kulaṃ piṇḍāya praviśati tatra tatraeva dvāre tūṣṇīṃ bhūtā asthātuatha khalu bhagavān etasmin nidāne etasmin prakaraṇe tasyāṃ velāyām imāṃ gāthām abhāṣatauabpūrvakeṇa nivāsena pratyutpannena tena caucdetena jāyate prema candrasya kumude yathāutasmāt tarhi bhikṣavo anabhisamitānāṃ caturṇām āryasatyānām abhisamayāyaadhimātraṃ vīryaṃ tīvracchando vīryaṃ śabdāpayāmiutsāha unnatir aprativāṇiḥ smṛtyā saṃprajanyena apramādato yogaḥ caraṇīyaḥ drutam eṣāṃ caturṇā duḥkhasyaāryasatyasya duḥkhasamudayanya nirodhasya nirodhagāminyāḥ pratipada āryasatyasya amīṣāṃ caturṇām āryasatyānām  anabhisamitānām abhisamayāyaadhimātraṃ tīvracchando vīryaṃ vyāyāma utsāha unnatir aprativāṇiḥ smṛtyā saṃprajanyenaapramādato yogaḥ karaṇīyaḥ up asmiṃś ca khalu punar dharmaparyāye bhāṣyamāṇe bhikṣūṇāṃ ṣaṣṭimātrāṇām anupādāyāsravebhyaś cittāni vimuktānisaṃbahulānāṃ śrāvakāṇāṃ brahmaṇāṃ gṛhapatīnaṃ ca virajaskaṃ vigatamalaṃ dharmacakṣur udapādi viśuddhaṃuidam avocad bhagavānāttamanasas te bhikṣavo bhagavato bhāṣitam abhyanandaniti śrīdivyāvadāne śārdūlakarṇāvadānaṃEnd
